                        <div data-reactid="1048">
                         This place is adorable. It has everything you need plus more, cafe, restaurants. The apartment is located downtown Long Beach and is 2 blocks from the beach, metro station to LA, marina and the Pike. Everything in this area is simply 2 blocks away.

                        <div data-reactid="1049">
                         The apartment is located on the corner of the building with so much natural light and views of the city. It is a beautifully hand decorated from A to Z space that provides an extra warm homey but modern feel. I am positive this place will mark your memory over the years. 
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1050">
                         It is a coffee culture neighborhood just like back in Europe where I am from. It feel. Really unique to live here. Besides we are 2 blocks from the beach, .3miles to Convention Center and walking distance to Catalina Ferry if you fancy seeing the Mediterranean of the West Coast. :)))

We had 4 people (2 couples) and it although it's a small space we didn't feel claustrophobic and there were enough personal touches to make you thankful to not be in a hotel room. Although there are 3 places to lay your head, only one bed is really comfortable for sleeping so it is probably ideal for 1 or 2 people. There is a neat little indoor/ outdoor common area where the laundry facilities are located, which was really nice. The neighborhood is amazing! Word of caution to peeps traveling with kids. The space is listed as family friendly, but unless you are the parent to children who's volume level never exceeds a 4 and activity level never rises above book reading, this might not be the best place. There is quite literally no room to play in or immediately around the building, so just be mindful of that when booking with kids. On the flip side, this property is in easy walking distance of the beach, beautiful parks, the aquarium, Seaside Village, a gazillion eateries, eclectic shops and a grocery store just around the corner.                          Completely remodeled, sunny, open, home in the East Village, with a spacious back yard. Centrally located only a .5 mile from the beach, metro and downtown. Dog friendly, walking distance to tons of great restaurants. It is a shared bathroom. Please read detail description.

                         We've recently remodeled our entire home, the greenest ways possible, as we both work from home, it's important to us to have a healthy space. Pets will incur an additional $10/night on top of the airbnb fee. Last minute bookers, unfortunately I do not take same day bookings as I have not had good experiences in the past. Please provide at least 48 hours notice out of courtesy. Production: we have been used at a production site for TV/commercials in the past. Production shoots start at $400/day. Please inquire via message!
